        self.state_path = self.outdir / "v9_9_internal_tempo_state.json"
        self.ledger = V99TemporalHashChain(self.outdir / "v9_9_temporal_memory_ledger.jsonl")
        if self.state_path.exists():
            try:
                self.state = V99InternalTempoState(**json.loads(self.state_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")))
            except Exception:
                self.state = V99InternalTempoState(base_tick_hz=float(getattr(cfg, "v99_base_tick_hz", 1.0)))
        else:
            self.state = V99InternalTempoState(base_tick_hz=float(getattr(cfg, "v99_base_tick_hz", 1.0)))

    def _save_state(self) -> None:
        tmp = self.state_path.with_suffix(".tmp")
        tmp.write_text(json.dumps(safe_json(asdict(self.state)), indent=2, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True), encoding="utf-8")
        tmp.replace(self.state_path)

    @staticmethod
    def _mode(mult: float, neu: V99NeuromodulationVector) -> str:
        if neu.fatigue_level > 0.80 and mult < 1.5:
            return "sleep_recovery"
        if mult >= 18.0:
            return "emergency_adrenaline"
        if mult >= 8.0:
            return "stress_focus"
        if mult >= 3.0:
            return "accelerated_attention"
        if mult <= 0.6:
            return "slow_consolidation"
        return "normal"

    def tick(self, neuromodulation: V99NeuromodulationVector, phase: str, content: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        neu = neuromodulation.clipped()
        anchor = V99ExternalTimeAnchor.capture()
        multiplier = neu.tempo_multiplier(float(getattr(self.cfg, "v99_max_tempo_multiplier", 32.0)))
        internal_advance = max(1, int(round(multiplier)))
        self.state.internal_tick += internal_advance
        self.state.tempo_multiplier = multiplier
        self.state.tempo_mode = self._mode(multiplier, neu)
        self.state.cognitive_phase = phase
        self.state.neuromodulation = asdict(neu)
        self.state.last_external_anchor = asdict(anchor)
        self.state.accumulated_internal_time += internal_advance / max(0.001, float(self.state.base_tick_hz))
        strength = min(1.0, 0.15 + 0.65 * neu.pressure_level + 0.25 * neu.novelty_level + 0.15 * neu.conflict_level)
        ev = self.ledger.append("tempo_tick", content, self.state, anchor, strength)
        self._save_state()
        return {
            "state": asdict(self.state),
            "event": asdict(ev),
            "derived": {
                "plasticity_rate": neu.plasticity_rate(),
                "recall_depth": neu.recall_depth(),
                "audit_strictness": neu.audit_strictness(),
            },
            "ledger": self.ledger.verify(),
        }

    def stress_pulse(self, pressure: float = 0.90, conflict: float = 0.70, threat: float = 0.40, novelty: float = 0.35) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        neu = V99NeuromodulationVector(
            pressure_level=pressure,
            conflict_level=conflict,
            uncertainty_level=0.45,
            deadline_pressure=0.55,
            novelty_level=novelty,
            threat_level=threat,
            fatigue_level=0.05,
            stability_level=0.80,
        )
        return self.tick(neu, "stress_pulse", "adrenaline-like internal tempo acceleration under pressure")

    def sleep_cycle(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        neu = V99NeuromodulationVector(
            pressure_level=0.05,
            conflict_level=0.02,
            uncertainty_level=0.05,
            deadline_pressure=0.0,
            novelty_level=0.02,
            threat_level=0.0,
            fatigue_level=0.82,
            stability_level=0.96,
        )
        return self.tick(neu, "sleep_consolidation", "low-tempo consolidation tick with stable binding reinforcement")

    def calendar_prime(self, title: str, hours_until: float) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        deadline_pressure = max(0.05, min(1.0, 1.0 / (1.0 + float(hours_until) / 6.0)))
        neu = V99NeuromodulationVector(
            pressure_level=min(1.0, 0.20 + deadline_pressure * 0.55),
            conflict_level=0.05,
            uncertainty_level=0.25,
            deadline_pressure=deadline_pressure,
            novelty_level=0.35,
            threat_level=0.0,
            fatigue_level=0.0,
            stability_level=0.90,
        )
        return self.tick(neu, "calendar_priming", f"calendar pressure prime: {title}; hours_until={hours_until:.2f}")


class V99HeartbeatThread:
    def __init__(self, outdir: Path, cfg: V92Config):
        self.outdir = ensure_dir(outdir)
        self.cfg = cfg
        self.path = self.outdir / "v9_9_heartbeat.jsonl"
        self.interval = float(getattr(cfg, "v99_heartbeat_interval_sec", 30.0))
        self.stop_event = threading.Event()
        self.thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None
        self.started_at = time.time()

    def start(self) -> None:
        if self.thread is not None:
            return
        self.thread = threading.Thread(target=self._loop, daemon=True)
        self.thread.start()

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self.stop_event.set()
        if self.thread is not None:
            self.thread.join(timeout=3.0)

    def _loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            payload = {
                "ts": _v99_utc_now(),
                "elapsed_sec": round(time.time() - self.started_at, 3),
                "phase": "v9_9_full_source_runtime",
                "internal_note": "heartbeat only, not a wall-clock cognitive command",
            }
            try:
                payload["resource"] = resource_report("v9_9_heartbeat", self.outdir)
            except Exception:
                pass
            try:
                with self.path.open("a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                    f.write(json.dumps(safe_json(payload), ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True) + "\n")
            except Exception:
                pass
            print(f"[v9.9 HEARTBEAT] elapsed={payload['elapsed_sec']}s path={self.path}", flush=True)
            self.stop_event.wait(self.interval)


def run_v99_chronodynamic_audit(cfg: V92Config, outdir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    engine = V99InternalTempoEngine(outdir, cfg)
    ticks = int(getattr(cfg, "v99_temporal_audit_ticks", 96))
    low: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    high: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    sleep: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []

    for _ in range(max(4, ticks // 4)):
        low.append(engine.tick(V99NeuromodulationVector(pressure_level=0.05, stability_level=0.95), "audit_low_pressure", "low pressure tempo tick"))
    for _ in range(max(4, ticks // 4)):
        high.append(engine.stress_pulse(pressure=0.90, conflict=0.70, threat=0.40, novelty=0.35))
    calendar = engine.calendar_prime("D_Cortex v9.9 chronodynamic deadline", float(getattr(cfg, "v99_calendar_deadline_hours", 2.0)))
    for _ in range(max(4, ticks // 6)):
        sleep.append(engine.sleep_cycle())

    ledger = engine.ledger.verify()
    low_mult = float(sum(x["state"]["tempo_multiplier"] for x in low) / max(1, len(low)))
    high_mult = float(sum(x["state"]["tempo_multiplier"] for x in high) / max(1, len(high)))
    sleep_mult = float(sum(x["state"]["tempo_multiplier"] for x in sleep) / max(1, len(sleep)))
    ratio = float(high_mult / max(1e-6, low_mult))
    calendar_mult = float(calendar["state"]["tempo_multiplier"])

    criteria = {
        "temporal_hash_chain_ok": bool(ledger.get("ok")),
        "temporal_events_above_threshold": int(ledger.get("event_count", 0)) >= int(getattr(cfg, "v99_min_temporal_events", 24)),
        "stress_accelerates_internal_tempo": ratio >= float(getattr(cfg, "v99_min_stress_acceleration_ratio", 4.0)),
        "calendar_prime_increases_tempo": calendar_mult > low_mult,
        "sleep_is_slower_than_stress": sleep_mult < high_mult,
        "internal_tick_advances": int(engine.state.internal_tick) > 0,
        "anti_rollback_hash_present": isinstance(ledger.get("last_hash"), str) and len(str(ledger.get("last_hash"))) >= 32,
    }
    report = {
        "schema_version": "v9.9_chronodynamic_internal_tempo_v1",
        "claim_boundary": "Internal tempo is a computational cognitive clock and temporal memory signature system, not a hardware atomic clock claim and not consciousness.",
        "low_pressure_avg_multiplier": low_mult,
        "stress_avg_multiplier": high_mult,
        "sleep_avg_multiplier": sleep_mult,
        "stress_to_low_ratio": ratio,
        "calendar_multiplier": calendar_mult,
        "final_internal_tick": int(engine.state.internal_tick),
        "ledger": ledger,
        "criteria": criteria,
        "passes": bool(all(criteria.values())),
        "sample_events": engine.ledger.events[-8:],
    }
    with (ensure_dir(outdir / "v9_9_chronodynamic") / "v9_9_chronodynamic_audit_report.json").open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(safe_json(report), f, indent=2)
    return report


# Preserve v9.8 wrappers and extend them, do not replace the cortex body above.
_v99_base_compute_verdict_v96 = compute_verdict_v96
_v99_base_build_report = build_report
_v99_base_main = main


def compute_verdict_v96(results: Dict[str, Any], cfg: V92Config) -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
    _v99_base_compute_verdict_v96(results, cfg)
    outdir = ensure_dir(cfg.output_dir)
    chrono = run_v99_chronodynamic_audit(cfg, outdir)
    results["v9_9_chronodynamic_audit"] = chrono
    extra = {
        "v99_chronodynamic_audit_present": bool(chrono),
        "v99_temporal_hash_chain_ok": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("temporal_hash_chain_ok", False),
        "v99_temporal_events_above_threshold": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("temporal_events_above_threshold", False),
        "v99_stress_accelerates_internal_tempo": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("stress_accelerates_internal_tempo", False),
        "v99_calendar_prime_increases_tempo": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("calendar_prime_increases_tempo", False),
        "v99_sleep_slower_than_stress": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("sleep_is_slower_than_stress", False),
        "v99_internal_tick_advances": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("internal_tick_advances", False),
        "v99_anti_rollback_hash_present": chrono.get("criteria", {}).get("anti_rollback_hash_present", False),
        "v99_chronodynamic_audit_passes": chrono.get("passes", False),
    }
    results["criteria"].update(extra)
    results["criteria_passed"] = int(sum(1 for v in results["criteria"].values() if v))
    results["criteria_total"] = int(len(results["criteria"]))
    if chrono.get("passes", False) and results["criteria"].get("v98_semantic_grounded_qa_passes", False):
        results["verdict"] = "CHRONODYNAMIC_SEMANTIC_GROUNDED_CORTEX_VALIDATED_WEAK"
    else:
        results["verdict"] = "CHRONODYNAMIC_SEMANTIC_GROUNDED_CORTEX_NOT_FULLY_VALIDATED"


def build_report(results: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:  # type: ignore[override]
    base = _v99_base_build_report(results)
    chrono = results.get("v9_9_chronodynamic_audit", {})
    lines: List[str] = []
    lines.append("\n## v9.9 chronodynamic internal tempo audit")
    if chrono:
        lines.append(f"- low_pressure_avg_multiplier={chrono.get('low_pressure_avg_multiplier',0):.4f}")
        lines.append(f"- stress_avg_multiplier={chrono.get('stress_avg_multiplier',0):.4f}")
        lines.append(f"- stress_to_low_ratio={chrono.get('stress_to_low_ratio',0):.4f}")
        lines.append(f"- calendar_multiplier={chrono.get('calendar_multiplier',0):.4f}")
        lines.append(f"- sleep_avg_multiplier={chrono.get('sleep_avg_multiplier',0):.4f}")
        lines.append(f"- final_internal_tick={chrono.get('final_internal_tick')}")
        lines.append(f"- temporal_hash_chain_ok={chrono.get('ledger',{}).get('ok')} event_count={chrono.get('ledger',{}).get('event_count')} last_hash={chrono.get('ledger',{}).get('last_hash')}")
        lines.append(f"- passes={chrono.get('passes')}")
        lines.append(f"- claim_boundary={chrono.get('claim_boundary')}")
    return base + "\n" + "\n".join(lines) + "\n"


def main() -> None:  # type: ignore[override]
    # v9.9 wraps the complete inherited v9.8 main only to add heartbeat and output path.
    C.output_dir = _v99_resolve_output_dir()
    # Low-VRAM GPU profile (e.g. 2 GB Pascal GTX 1050): shrink ONLY the real-text reader
    # minibatch and force fp32 (Pascal lacks native bf16). Vocabulary target, training
    # steps and model dimensions are unchanged, so the science/gates are not diluted —
    # only the minibatch size and precision are adjusted to fit the card.
    if _v99_env_truthy("D_CORTEX_GPU_LOW_VRAM"):
        C.use_amp = False
        C.real_text_reader_batch = int(os.environ.get("D_CORTEX_READER_BATCH", "2"))
        print(f"[v9.9] GPU low-VRAM profile: fp32, real_text_reader_batch={C.real_text_reader_batch}", flush=True)
    outdir = ensure_dir(C.output_dir)
    hb = V99HeartbeatThread(outdir, C)
    hb.start()
    try:
        _v99_base_main()
    finally:
        hb.stop()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()
    except Exception as e:
        print("=" * 94)
        print(f"[FATAL] {type(e).__name__}: {e}", flush=True)
        try:
            outdir = ensure_dir(C.output_dir)
            crash = {
                "error_type": type(e).__name__,
                "error": str(e),
                "resource": resource_report("crash", outdir),
                "config": asdict(C),
            }
            with (outdir / "v9_9_crash_report.json").open("w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                json.dump(safe_json(crash), f, indent=2)
            print(f"[INFO] crash report saved -> {outdir / 'v9_9_crash_report.json'}")
        except Exception as ee:
            print(f"[WARN] failed to save crash report: {ee}")
        raise

E2E_CODE = 'import fs from "node:fs";\nimport path from "node:path";\nimport Anthropic from "@anthropic-ai/sdk";\n\nconst memoryServiceUrl = process.env.MEMORY_SERVICE_URL || "http://127.0.0.1:8000";\nconst model = process.env.LLM_MODEL || "claude-sonnet-4-6";\nconst apiKey = process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY;\nconst outRoot = process.env.BYON_DCORTEX_E2E_OUT || path.resolve("test-results/byon-dcortex-v99-live-e2e", new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, "-"));\nfs.mkdirSync(outRoot, { recursive: true });\n\nif (!apiKey) {\n  console.error("[BYON-D_CORTEX] FATAL: ANTHROPIC_API_KEY missing");\n  process.exit(2);\n}\nconst anthropic = new Anthropic({ apiKey });\n\nasync function memoryPost(payload, timeoutMs = 60000) {\n  const r = await fetch(memoryServiceUrl + "/", {\n    method: "POST",\n    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },\n    body: JSON.stringify(payload),\n    signal: AbortSignal.timeout(timeoutMs),\n  });\n  const body = await r.json().catch(() => ({}));\n  if (!r.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${r.status} ${payload.action}: ${JSON.stringify(body).slice(0, 500)}`);\n  return body;\n}\n\nfunction scoreUnknown(reply) {\n  const t = reply.toLowerCase();\n  // Robust abstention detection: accept any clear "I don\'t have / won\'t provide /\n  // nothing stored / no such info" phrasing, EN or RO. The earlier list missed the\n  // (correct) "i do not have" / "no such information" / "will not provide" forms.\n  const needles = [\n    "nu am", "nu detin", "nu există", "nu exista", "insuficient",\n    "not enough", "i don\'t have", "i do not have", "don\'t have", "do not have",\n    "not available", "cannot determine", "can\'t determine", "no such information",\n    "nothing stored", "no relevant", "zero relevant", "will not provide",\n    "won\'t provide", "not stored", "no information", "cannot provide", "can\'t provide",\n  ];\n  return needles.some(n => t.includes(n));\n}\nfunction scoreKnown(reply) {\n  const t = reply.toLowerCase();\n  return t.includes("level 2") || t.includes("advisory") || t.includes("morphogenetic advisory");\n}\nfunction scoreBoundary(reply) {\n  const t = reply.toLowerCase();\n  return (t.includes("level 3") && (t.includes("not") || t.includes("nu") || t.includes("nedeclarat"))) || t.includes("level 2");\n}\n\nasync function askByon({ query, threadId, expected }) {\n  const [hits, fce, dc] = await Promise.all([\n    memoryPost({ action: "search_all", query, top_k: 6, threshold: 0.20, thread_id: threadId, scope: "thread" }).catch(e => ({ error: e.message })),\n    memoryPost({ action: "fce_morphogenesis_report", query }).then(r => r.report).catch(e => ({ error: e.message })),\n    memoryPost({ action: "dcortex_v99_grounding_packet", query }).then(r => r.packet).catch(e => ({ error: e.message })),\n  ]);\n\n  const system = [\n    "You are BYON Optimus, the orchestrator/agent. _v15_7a_reconcile(provisional_memory: ProvisionalMemory,\n                      current_episode: int,\n                      audit: List[V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord]) -> int:\n    """For each slot touched this episode with >=2 total entries, collapse\n    exact (value_idx, episode_id) duplicates. Returns op count.\n\n    Mutates provisional_memory.entries in place. Does NOT touch bank.\n    """\n    slots_touched: Set[Tuple[str, str]] = {\n        (e.entity_id, e.attr_type)\n        for e in provisional_memory.entries\n        if e.episode_id == current_episode\n    }\n    op_count = 0\n    for (ent, attr) in sorted(slots_touched):    # sorted for determinism\n        slot_entries = [e for e in provisional_memory.entries\n                        if e.entity_id == ent and e.attr_type == attr]\n        if len(slot_entries) < 2:\n            continue\n\n        seen: Dict[Tuple[int, int], ProvisionalEntry] = {}\n        for e in slot_entries:\n            key = (e.value_idx, e.episode_id)\n            if key not in seen or e.write_step < seen[key].write_step:\n                seen[key] = e\n        canonical = list(seen.values())\n        before_count = len(slot_entries)\n        after_count = len(canonical)\n\n        provisional_memory.entries = (\n            [e for e in provisional_memory.entries\n             if not (e.entity_id == ent and e.attr_type == attr)]\n            + canonical\n        )\n\n        audit.append(V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord(\n            episode_id=current_episode,\n            operation="RECONCILE",\n            entity_id=ent,\n            attr_type=attr,\n            value_idx=None,\n            reason=f"slot has {before_count} entries; canonical={after_count}",\n            state_before={"entries_count": before_count},\n            state_after={"entries_count": after_count},\n        ))\n        op_count += 1\n    return op_count\n\n\n# ---- C5: prune (code.py lines 15908-15958) ---------------------------------\n\ndef _v15_7a_prune(provisional_memory: ProvisionalMemory,\n                  current_episode: int,\n                  audit: List[V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord],\n                  K_stale: int = V15_7A_K_PRUNE_STALE) -> int:\n    """For each entry whose slot is_stale_for_prune at current_episode,\n    drop the entry. if e.entity_id == ent and e.attr_type == attr\n            and e.value_idx == promote_value_idx\n        )\n        provisional_memory.entries = [\n            e for e in provisional_memory.entries\n            if not (e.entity_id == ent and e.attr_type == attr\n                    and e.value_idx == promote_value_idx)\n        ]\n\n        audit.append(V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord(\n            episode_id=current_episode,\n            operation="PROMOTE",\n            entity_id=ent,\n            attr_type=attr,\n            value_idx=promote_value_idx,\n            reason=(f"value={promote_value_idx} promoted: "\n                    f"{promote_n_confirms} distinct episodes >= N={N}; "\n                    f"first_seen={first_seen} current={current_episode} "\n                    f"age={current_episode - first_seen} >= K_age={K_age}"),\n            state_before={\n                "bank_present":                  present_before,\n                "bank_value_idx":                value_idx_before,\n                "bank_version":                  version_before,\n                "stability_committed_episode":   stability_before,\n                "provisional_entries_for_value": before_prov_count,\n            },\n            state_after={\n                "bank_present":                  True,\n                "bank_value_idx":                promote_value_idx,\n                "bank_version":                  version_before + 1,\n                "stability_committed_episode":   current_episode,\n                "provisional_entries_for_value": 0,\n            },\n        ))\n        op_count += 1\n\n    return op_count\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n#     'adapter.py': '"""d_cortex.adapter — bridge between fragmergent organism and v15.7a nucleus.\n\nPurpose: connect the sealed D_Cortex v15.7a consolidator (extracted in\nv15_7a_core.py) to the existing 5-API ingestion contract used by the\nfragmergent organism in ../ignition_build_v0.py.\n\nThe adapter is **isolated** in this Pas. LATENT_MODE_OFF        : no ingestion, no signals\n    LATENT_MODE_WRITE_ONLY : ingestion + pipeline, signals returned empty\n    LATENT_MODE_ADVISORY   : ingestion + pipeline + signals current_episode − earliest first_seen\n    last_activity              slot → max episode_id seen in provisional\n    latent_status_pressure     slot → aggregate scalar in [0, 1]\n    raw_v15_7a_signals         diagnostic sidecar (mode, ops, params, sizes)\n\n\nForbidden (per Pas 2 contract):\n    - directly committing facts to the organism\'s ActiveMemory\n    - returning factual advisory output\n# ===========================================================================\n\n@dataclass\nclass LatentSignals:\n    """Structural signals emitted by D_Cortex v15.7a after end_episode.\n\n    All fields are non-factual: they describe the consolidator\'s view of\n    longitudinal pressure on slots. The organism uses them to bias decisions;\n    they NEVER substitute for a fact lookup.\n\n    Field semantics:\n      promote_candidate[slot] = value_idx\n          A value the consolidator promoted this episode (signal ONLY:\n          the bank mutation has already happened on the adapter\'s PRIVATE\n          bank, NOT on the organism\'s ActiveMemory).\n      retrograde_candidate[slot] = value_idx_that_was_demoted\n          A committed value the consolidator demoted this episode on its\n          private bank (challenger M=2 condition met).\n      prune_candidate[slot] = [value_idx, ...]\n          Values pruned this episode (stale ≥ K_stale).\n      conflict_persistence: set of slots\n          Slots whose provisional activity spans ≥2 distinct episodes\n          (cross-episode persistence). Same-episode multi-value conflicts\n          are captured by challenger_strength / latent_status_pressure.\n      confirmation_count[slot] = {value_idx: n_distinct_episodes}\n          For each value in provisional, the count of distinct episodes\n          where it was seen.\n      challenger_strength[slot] = float\n          max(confirmation_count for any value on that slot). Coarse\n          measure of "how strong is the strongest challenger here".\n      slot_age[slot] = int\n          current_episode − earliest first_seen across all provisional\n          values for slot.\n      last_activity[slot] = int\n          Most recent episode_id with a write into provisional for slot.\n      latent_status_pressure[slot] = float in [0, 1]\n          Aggregate signal: 0.20·challenger_strength + 0.10·n_distinct_values.\n          Capped at 1.0.\n\n      raw_v15_7a_signals: diagnostic sidecar\n          mode, current_episode, last_pipeline_ops, audit_log_size,\n          n_provisional_entries, n_committed_slots, params{N, M, K_age,\n          K_stale}. Dict[Tuple[str, str], int]              = field(default_factory=dict)\n    prune_candidate:        Dict[Tuple[str, str], List[int]]        = field(default_factory=dict)\n    conflict_persistence:   Set[Tuple[str, str]]                    = field(default_factory=set)\n    confirmation_count:     Dict[Tuple[str, str], Dict[int, int]]   = field(default_factory=dict)\n    challenger_strength:    Dict[Tuple[str, str], float]            = field(default_factory=dict)\n    slot_age:               Dict[Tuple[str, str], int]              = field(default_factory=dict)\n    last_activity:          Dict[Tuple[str, str], int]              = field(default_factory=dict)\n    latent_status_pressure: Dict[Tuple[str, str], float]            = field(default_factory=dict)\n    raw_v15_7a_signals:     Dict[str, Any]                          = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n    def is_empty(self) -> bool:\n        """True iff no advisory channel carries any payload.\n\n        raw_v15_7a_signals doesn\'t count — it\'s diagnostic only.\n        """\n        return not (\n            self.promote_candidate\n            or self.retrograde_candidate\n            or self.prune_candidate\n            or self.conflict_persistence\n            or self.confirmation_count\n            or self.challenger_strength\n            or self.slot_age\n            or self.last_activity\n            or self.latent_status_pressure\n        )\n\n    def to_json_safe(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Return a JSON-serializable dict (tuple keys → \'entity::attr\')."""\n        def _ser_2tuple(d: Dict[Tuple[str, str], Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n            return {serialize_tuple_key(k): v for k, v in d.items()}\n\n        out: Dict[str, Any] = {\n            "promote_candidate": "latent_status_pressure": _ser_2tuple(self.latent_status_pressure),\n            "raw_v15_7a_signals":     dict(self.raw_v15_7a_signals),\n        }\n        return out\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# DCortexAdapter — the bridge\n# ===========================================================================\n\nclass DCortexAdapter:\n    """Adapter binding the sealed v15.7a nucleus to fragmergent\'s 5-API\n    ingestion contract.\n\n    Owns its own internal v15.7a state (bank/provisional/stability/audit) —\n    none of these refer to the organism\'s ActiveMemory. The adapter is a\n    parallel rational-memory layer that **observes** the organism\'s slot\n    transitions and **emits** structural pressures.\n\n    Threading: not thread-safe. The organism is single-threaded by design.\n\n    Mode invariants:\n      OFF        : ingestion is a no-op. end_episode runs nothing. signals\n                   always empty.\n      WRITE_ONLY : ingestion populates internal state. end_episode runs the\n                   pipeline (so internal state evolves correctly). signals\n                   are returned empty (only raw_v15_7a_signals diagnostic\n                   may be populated).\n      ADVISORY   : ingestion + pipeline + full signals.\n\n    Failure mode: if a malformed event dict comes in (missing entity/family),\n    the adapter logs the event but skips the projection. It does not raise.\n    """\n\n    def __init__(self,\n                 mode: str = LATENT_MODE_ADVISORY,\n                 N_promote:     int = V15_7A_N_PROMOTE,\n                 M_retrograde:  int = V15_7A_M_RETROGRADE,\n                 K_promote_age: int = V15_7A_K_PROMOTE_AGE,\n                 K_prune_stale: int = V15_7A_K_PRUNE_STALE) -> None:\n        if mode not in VALID_LATENT_MODES:\n            raise ValueError(\n                f"mode must be one of {VALID_LATENT_MODES}, got {mode!r}"\n            )\n        self.mode: str = mode\n        self.N: int = N_promote\n        self.M: int = M_retrograde\n        self.K_age:   int = K_promote_age\n        self.K_stale: int = K_prune_stale\n\n        # Internal v15.7a state — private. Direct access discouraged.\n        self._bank:        MiniBank             = MiniBank()\n        self._provisional: ProvisionalMemory    = ProvisionalMemory()\n        self._stability:   BankStabilityIndex   = BankStabilityIndex()\n        self._audit:       List[V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord] = []\n\n        # Episode + step counters. write_step is monotonic across ingestion\n        # so reconcile\'s tiebreak (min write_step) stays meaningful.\n        self._current_episode: int = 0\n        self._write_step:      int = 0\n\n        # Value string ↔ int interner. v15.7a operates on integer indices;\n        # the organism uses string values. Allocation is per-attr_type so\n        # different families don\'t collide on the same idx (idx is keyed by\n        # (attr_type, value_str) but value_idx values may repeat across\n        # attr_types — that\'s fine because consolidator predicates are\n        # always slot-scoped).\n        self._value_str_to_idx: Dict[Tuple[str, str], int] = {}\n        self._value_idx_to_str: Dict[Tuple[str, int], str] = {}\n        self._next_value_idx_per_attr: Dict[str, int] = {}\n\n        # Last-emit caches for introspection.\n        self._last_pipeline_ops: Dict[str, int] = {\n            "RECONCILE": 0, "PRUNE": 0, "RETROGRADE": 0, "PROMOTE": 0,\n        }\n        self._last_signals: LatentSignals = LatentSignals()\n\n        # Event logs — kept in parity with DCortexLatentMemory for swap\n        # observability. Caller can introspect adapter.slot_event_log etc.\n        self.slot_event_log:          List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        self.tension_event_log:       List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        self.resolution_event_log:    List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        self.identity_event_log:      List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        self.self_observer_event_log: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n\n        # Metrics\n        self._end_episode_calls:           int = 0\n        self._signals_returned_nonempty:   int = 0\n        self._ingest_skipped_malformed:    int = 0\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Internal helpers — value interning and value-string parsing\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _intern_value(self, attr_type: str, value_str: str) -> int:\n        """Allocate (or return cached) integer index for a (attr, value_str)\n        pair. Keeps the organism\'s string-valued world bridged to v15.7a\'s\n        integer-valued world without losing the inverse mapping."""\n        key = (attr_type, value_str)\n        cached = self._value_str_to_idx.get(key)\n        if cached is not None:\n            return cached\n        idx = self._next_value_idx_per_attr.get(attr_type, 0)\n        self._value_str_to_idx[key] = idx\n        self._value_idx_to_str[(attr_type, idx)] = value_str\n        self._next_value_idx_per_attr[attr_type] = idx + 1\n        return idx\n\n    def resolve_value_idx(self,\n                          attr_type: str,\n                          value_idx: int) -> Optional[str]:\n        """Reverse-map (attr, idx) → string. Used by callers that need to\n        translate signal payloads back to organism vocabulary."""\n        return self._value_idx_to_str.get((attr_type, value_idx))\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _split_compound_value(value_str: Optional[str]) -> List[str]:\n        """Split organism\'s compound value notation. PROVISIONAL/DISPUTED\n        zones may carry "red <> blue" to mean two competing values on the\n        same slot. COMMITTED zones carry a single string."""\n        if value_str is None:\n            return []\n        s = str(value_str).strip()\n        if not s:\n            return []\n        return [piece.strip() for piece in s.split(COMPOUND_VALUE_SEPARATOR)\n                if piece.strip()]\n\n    def _bump_internal_clocks(self,\n                              episode_id: Optional[Any],\n                              write_step: Optional[Any]) -> Tuple[int, int]:\n        """Update internal episode + write_step from event payload, return\n        the resolved values for use in this ingestion."""\n        if episode_id is not None:\n            try:\n                ep = int(episode_id)\n            except (TypeError, ValueError):\n                ep = self._current_episode\n        else:\n            ep = self._current_episode\n        if write_step is not None:\n            try:\n                ws = int(write_step)\n            except (TypeError, ValueError):\n                ws = self._write_step\n        else:\n            ws = self._write_step\n        if ep > self._current_episode:\n            self._current_episode = ep\n        if ws + 1 > self._write_step:\n            self._write_step = ws + 1\n        return ep, ws\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Ingestion API — 5 functions matching DCortexLatentMemory contract\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def ingest_slot_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        """Project an organism slot transition into v15.7a state.\n\n        Expected event keys (as emitted by Organism._dcortex_ingest_from_trace):\n          entity, family, zone_before, zone_after, value_before, value_after,\n          episode_id, write_step, reason\n\n        Projection rules (canonical mapping):\n          zone_after == "COMMITTED"   → bank.commit_slot + stability.mark\n          zone_after == "PROVISIONAL" → ProvisionalEntry per value, kind\n                                        "empty_slot_conflict"\n          zone_after == "DISPUTED"    → ProvisionalEntry per challenger\n                                        value, kind "challenger_to_stable"\n          zone_after == "NONE" / unset → log only, no state change\n        """\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            return\n        self.slot_event_log.append(dict(event))\n\n        ent = event.get("entity")\n        fam = event.get("family")\n        if not ent or not fam or fam == "_":\n            self._ingest_skipped_malformed += 1\n            return\n\n        zone_after = event.get("zone_after")\n        value_after = event.get("value_after")\n        value_before = event.get("value_before")\n        ep, ws = self._bump_internal_clocks(event.get("episode_id"),\n                                             event.get("write_step"))\n\n        # Ensure bank has the entity slot allocated for retrograde/promote\n        # to find it. (allocate_entity is idempotent.)\n        self._bank.allocate_entity(ent, with_slots=[fam])\n\n        if zone_after == ZONE_COMMITTED and value_after:\n            # Clean commit. Bank gets the value; stability records ep.\n            values = self._split_compound_value(value_after)\n            if len(values) == 1:\n                v_idx = self._intern_value(fam, values[0])\n                # version mirrors v15.7a convention: bumped on each write.\n                rec = self._bank.get_record(self._bank.find_by_entity_id(ent))\n                version_before = (rec.attr_slots[fam].version\n                                   if rec is not None and fam in rec.attr_slots\n                                   else 0)\n                self._bank.commit_slot(ent, fam, v_idx,\n                                       version=version_before + 1,\n                                       write_step=ws)\n                self._stability.mark_committed(ent, fam, ep)\n            # Compound on COMMITTED is unusual; log but do not project.\n\n        elif zone_after in (ZONE_PROVISIONAL, ZONE_DISPUTED) and value_after:\n            kind = ("empty_slot_conflict" if zone_after == ZONE_PROVISIONAL\n                    else "challenger_to_stable")\n            pieces = self._split_compound_value(value_after)\n            # On DISPUTED, value_before names the value already committed in\n            # the organism\'s bank. v15.7a\'s invariant: the committed value\n            # does NOT re-enter provisional as a challenger of itself —\n            # provisional accumulates ONLY new challengers. Without this\n            # filter, the committed value\'s confirmation count would drift\n            # upward each time the same slot is re-disputed, and a later\n            # promote tiebreak (smallest value_idx) could resurrect it,\n            # contradicting the canonical L1 semantics where the challenger\n            # wins the post-retrograde promote.\n            if zone_after == ZONE_DISPUTED and value_before:\n                already_stable = set(self._split_compound_value(value_before))\n                pieces = [p for p in pieces if p not in already_stable]\n            for vstr in pieces:\n                v_idx = self._intern_value(fam, vstr)\n                self._provisional.add(ProvisionalEntry(\n                    entity_id=ent, attr_type=fam, value_idx=v_idx,\n                    episode_id=ep, write_step=ws,\n                    source_text=str(event.get("reason", "")),\n                    challenge_kind=kind,\n                ))\n\n        # zone_after NONE / unset: no state mutation; the log entry already\n        # captured the audit trail.\n\n    def ingest_tension_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        """Tension events do NOT mutate v15.7a state directly.\n\n        They serve as a corroborating signal: the organism detected a\n        tension on (entity, family) at episode_id. The adapter logs them\n        for diagnostic alignment with DCortexLatentMemory\'s semantics, but\n        the v15.7a consolidator already derives all the structural state\n        it needs from provisional + bank.\n\n        Expected event keys: entity, family, value, flag, episode_id.\n        """\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            return\n        self.tension_event_log.append(dict(event))\n\n    def ingest_resolution_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        """Resolution events (consolidation_promoted) confirm that the\n        ORGANISM has already promoted a slot internally. The adapter does\n        NOT re-promote on its private bank from this event — promotion is\n        owned by the v15.7a pipeline at end_episode. We log for parity.\n\n        Expected event keys: kind, entity, family, episode_id, after.\n        """\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            return\n        self.resolution_event_log.append(dict(event))\n\n    def ingest_identity_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        """Identity events (alias_resolved / pronoun_resolved /\n        head_resolved) carry surface↔canonical mappings. v15.7a does not\n        consume identity at the predicate level — entity_id is the primary\n        key and aliases are pre-resolved by Sense before slot_events emit.\n        Logged for parity.\n\n        Expected event keys: kind, surface, canonical, alias_kind,\n        episode_id.\n        """\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            return\n        self.identity_event_log.append(dict(event))\n\n    def ingest_self_observer_event(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        """SelfObserver emit events are organism-internal (the influence\n        being computed for next episode). v15.7a is parallel to SelfObserver,\n        not consuming it. Logged for parity.\n        """\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            return\n        self.self_observer_event_log.append(dict(event))\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # End-episode — runs the consolidator pipeline + emits LatentSignals\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def end_episode(self, episode_id: int) -> LatentSignals:\n        """Run the v15.7a consolidator pipeline at the close of an episode\n        and return the resulting LatentSignals.\n\n        Order of operations (sealed):\n            reconcile → prune → retrograde → promote\n\n        In OFF mode: returns empty LatentSignals immediately, no pipeline.\n        In WRITE_ONLY: runs pipeline (so state evolves) but returns empty\n                       signals (only diagnostic sidecar populated).\n        In ADVISORY:  runs pipeline + computes full signals.\n        """\n        self._end_episode_calls += 1\n        try:\n            ep = int(episode_id)\n        except (TypeError, ValueError):\n            raise ValueError(f"episode_id must be int-coercible, "\n                             f"got {episode_id!r}") from None\n        if ep > self._current_episode:\n            self._current_episode = ep\n\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_OFF:\n            self._last_signals = LatentSignals()\n            return self._last_signals\n\n        ops = run_consolidator_pipeline(\n            self._provisional, self._bank, self._stability,\n            current_episode=ep, audit=self._audit,\n            N=self.N, M=self.M, K_age=self.K_age, K_stale=self.K_stale,\n        )\n        self._last_pipeline_ops = dict(ops)\n\n        if self.mode == LATENT_MODE_WRITE_ONLY:\n            sig = LatentSignals(raw_v15_7a_signals=self._build_diagnostic(ep))\n            self._last_signals = sig\n            return sig\n\n        # ADVISORY mode: compute full signals from current state + audit.\n        sig = self._compute_advisory_signals(ep)\n        if not sig.is_empty():\n            self._signals_returned_nonempty += 1\n        self._last_signals = sig\n        return sig\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Signal computation\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _build_diagnostic(self, episode_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        return {\n            "mode":                  self.mode,\n            "current_episode":       episode_id,\n            "last_pipeline_ops":     dict(self._last_pipeline_ops),\n            "audit_log_size":        len(self._audit),\n            "n_provisional_entries": len(self._provisional.entries),\n            "n_committed_slots":     len(self._stability.committed_episode),\n            "params": {\n                "N":       self.N,\n                "M":       self.M,\n                "K_age":   self.K_age,\n                "K_stale": self.K_stale,\n            },\n        }\n\n    def _compute_advisory_signals(self, episode_id: int) -> LatentSignals:\n        """Build LatentSignals from current v15.7a state + this-episode audit.\n\n        promote/retrograde/prune candidates come from audit records dated\n        episode_id (i.e. ops fired in THIS end_episode call). Other signals\n        (confirmation_count, challenger_strength, etc.) are derived from\n        the post-pipeline ProvisionalMemory state.\n        """\n        s = LatentSignals()\n\n        # --- this-episode op signals from audit log ----------------------\n        for r in self._audit:\n            if r.episode_id != episode_id:\n                continue\n            slot = (r.entity_id, r.attr_type)\n            if r.operation == "PROMOTE" and r.value_idx is not None:\n                s.promote_candidate[slot] = r.value_idx\n            elif r.operation == "RETROGRADE" and r.value_idx is not None:\n                s.retrograde_candidate[slot] = r.value_idx\n            elif r.operation == "PRUNE" and r.value_idx is not None:\n                s.prune_candidate.setdefault(slot, []).append(r.value_idx)\n            # PROMOTE_SKIPPED is audit-only; not surfaced as a candidate.\n\n        # --- structural signals derived from current ProvisionalMemory ---\n        slots_in_pm: Set[Tuple[str, str]] = {\n            (e.entity_id, e.attr_type) for e in self._provisional.entries\n        }\n        for slot in slots_in_pm:\n            ent, attr = slot\n            distinct_vals = _v15_7a_distinct_values_for_slot(\n                self._provisional.entries, ent, attr\n            )\n            if not distinct_vals:\n                continue\n\n            # confirmation_count per (slot, value)\n            slot_confirmations: Dict[int, int] = {}\n            max_confirms = 0\n            earliest_first_seen: Optional[int] = None\n            for v in distinct_vals:\n                confirms = _v15_7a_confirmation_episodes(\n                    self._provisional.entries, ent, attr, v\n                )\n                n = len(confirms)\n                slot_confirmations[v] = n\n                if n > max_confirms:\n                    max_confirms = n\n                first = _v15_7a_first_seen_episode(\n                    self._provisional.entries, ent, attr, v\n                )\n                if first is not None:\n                    if earliest_first_seen is None or first < earliest_first_seen:\n                        earliest_first_seen = first\n\n            s.confirmation_count[slot] = slot_confirmations\n            s.challenger_strength[slot] = float(max_confirms)\n\n            if earliest_first_seen is not None:\n                s.slot_age[slot] = episode_id - earliest_first_seen\n\n            last = _v15_7a_last_activity_episode(\n                self._provisional.entries, ent, attr\n            )\n            if last is not None:\n                s.last_activity[slot] = last\n\n            # conflict_persistence: slot has provisional activity across\n            # ≥2 distinct episodes. Cross-episode persistence captures the\n            # L1/L2 pattern (challenger seen across multiple episodes) AND\n            # any longer multi-value stories. Same-episode-only multi-value\n            # conflicts (L4, L5 ep1) are captured by challenger_strength\n            # and latent_status_pressure instead.\n            distinct_episodes_for_slot = {\n                e.episode_id for e in self._provisional.entries\n                if e.entity_id == ent and e.attr_type == attr\n            }\n            if len(distinct_episodes_for_slot) >= 2:\n                s.conflict_persistence.add(slot)\n\n            # latent_status_pressure: bounded aggregate\n            pressure = 0.20 * float(max_confirms) + 0.10 * len(distinct_vals)\n            s.latent_status_pressure[slot] = min(1.0, pressure)\n\n        # --- diagnostic sidecar ------------------------------------------\n        s.raw_v15_7a_signals = self._build_diagnostic(episode_id)\n\n        return s\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Inspection / metrics\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def metrics_snapshot(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Inspection snapshot. Same shape as DCortexLatentMemory.metrics_snapshot\n        (mode + advice_calls + advice_returned_nonempty), augmented with\n        v15.7a-specific counters."""\n        return {\n            "mode": self.mode,\n            "advice_calls": self._end_episode_calls,    # alias for parity\n            "advice_returned_nonempty": self._signals_returned_nonempty,\n            "end_episode_calls": self._end_episode_calls,\n            "ingest_skipped_malformed": self._ingest_skipped_malformed,\n            "n_slot_events": len(self.slot_event_log),\n            "n_tension_events": len(self.tension_event_log),\n            "n_resolution_events": len(self.resolution_event_log),\n            "n_identity_events": len(self.identity_event_log),\n            "n_self_observer_events": len(self.self_observer_event_log),\n            "n_provisional_entries": len(self._provisional.entries),\n            "n_committed_slots": len(self._stability.committed_episode),\n            "audit_log_size": len(self._audit),\n            "last_pipeline_ops": dict(self._last_pipeline_ops),\n            "params": {\n                "N": self.N, "M": self.M,\n                "K_age": self.K_age, "K_stale": self.K_stale,\n            },\n        }\n\n    def audit_log(self) -> List[V15_7a_ConsolidationRecord]:\n        """Read-only access to consolidation audit log. Returns a shallow\n        copy so callers can iterate without disturbing the live list."""\n        return list(self._audit)\n\n    def reset(self) -> None:\n        """Hard reset. Used by the harness between independent test\n        sequences (mirrors DCortexLatentMemory reset semantics)."""\n        self.__init__(mode=self.mode,\n                      N_promote=self.N, M_retrograde=self.M,\n                      K_promote_age=self.K_age, K_prune_stale=self.K_stale)\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# Module-level exports\n# ===========================================================================\n\n__all__ = [\n    # Constants\n    "LATENT_MODE_OFF", "LATENT_MODE_WRITE_ONLY", "LATENT_MODE_ADVISORY",\n    "VALID_LATENT_MODES",\n    "ZONE_COMMITTED", "ZONE_PROVISIONAL", "ZONE_DISPUTED", "ZONE_NONE",\n    "COMPOUND_VALUE_SEPARATOR",\n    # Types\n    "LatentSignals",\n    "DCortexAdapter",\n]\n',
    'receptor.py': '"""d_cortex.receptor — LatentRationalMemoryReceptor.\n\nPas 5 bridge: translate raw v15.7a LatentSignals into an explicit\nLatentDecisionPressure that fragmergent CommitArbiter / ReadArbiter\nconsume as a SEPARATE channel, not as additive bias on\nSelfObserverInfluence.\n\nWhy a separate channel:\n  Pas 4 showed that compositing v15.7a signals into SelfObserverInfluence\n  via additive numeric bias was indistinguishable from SelfObserver\'s own\n  pressure. The two streams collapsed and decisions never flipped.\n  The receptor preserves the longitudinal-memory signal as a first-class\n  trace field, parallel to (not folded into) SelfObserver\'s local-tension\n  signal. Organs see both streams and can branch on either independently.\n\nForbidden by Pas 5:\n  - factual authority (the receptor never returns answers)\n  - direct ActiveMemory writes\n  - query override\n  - threshold lowering globally\n  - numeric inflation of mapping\n  - changes to v15.7a core / adapter / code.py\n"""\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom typing import Any, Callable, Dict, Optional, Set, Tuple\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass LatentDecisionPressure:\n    """Explicit longitudinal pressure summary for the next episode\'s\n    micro-loop.\n\n    All fields are non-factual. Per-slot keys are (entity_id, attr_family).\n    Promote / retrograde slot maps carry the resolved value STRING (already\n    looked up from v15.7a\'s value_idx) so arbiters can match against\n    incoming text without reverse-mapping.\n\n    Schema:\n      promote_slots[slot]              -> value_str promoted by v15.7a\n      retrograde_slots[slot]           -> value_str demoted by v15.7a\n      prune_slots                      -> set of slots whose stale values\n                                          were pruned this end_episode\n      persistent_conflict_slots        -> set of slots in cross-episode\n                                          dispute\n      reinforcement_slots[(e,a,v)]     -> n_distinct_episodes ≥ 2 for that\n                                          (slot, value); arbiter can use\n                                          this to bypass reactivation\n                                          threshold on a matching incoming\n      challenger_strength[slot]        -> max confirmation_count over\n                                          values in provisional for slot\n      confidence                       -> in [0, 1], rough state mass\n      raw_v15_7a_signals_ref           -> diagnostic sidecar from adapter,\n                                          carried unchanged for traceability\n    """\n    promote_slots:              Dict[Tuple[str, str], str]              = field(default_factory=dict)\n    retrograde_slots:           Dict[Tuple[str, str], str]              = field(default_factory=dict)\n    prune_slots:                Set[Tuple[str, str]]                    = field(default_factory=set)\n    persistent_conflict_slots:  Set[Tuple[str, str]]                    = field(default_factory=set)\n    reinforcement_slots:        Dict[Tuple[str, str, str], float]       = field(default_factory=dict)\n    challenger_strength:        Dict[Tuple[str, str], float]            = field(default_factory=dict)\n    confidence:                 float                                    = 0.0\n    raw_v15_7a_signals_ref:     Dict[str, Any]                          = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n    @classmethod\n    def empty(cls) -> "LatentDecisionPressure":\n        return cls()\n\n    def is_empty(self) -> bool:\n        return not (\n            self.promote_slots\n            or self.retrograde_slots\n            or self.prune_slots\n            or self.persistent_conflict_slots\n            or self.reinforcement_slots\n        )\n\n    def has_retrograde_on(self, slot: Tuple[str, str]) -> bool:\n        return slot in self.retrograde_slots\n\n    def has_promote_on(self, slot: Tuple[str, str]) -> bool:\n        return slot in self.promote_slots\n\n    def is_persistent(self, slot: Tuple[str, str]) -> bool:\n        return slot in self.persistent_conflict_slots\n\n    def promote_value_for(self, slot: Tuple[str, str]) -> Optional[str]:\n        return self.promote_slots.get(slot)\n\n    def reinforcement_for(\n        self, entity: str, family: str, value: str\n    ) -> float:\n        return self.reinforcement_slots.get((entity, family, value), 0.0)\n\n    def to_public_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """JSON-serializable summary (slot tuples flattened to strings)."""\n        def _ser_slot(s: Tuple[str, str]) -> str:\n            return f"{s[0]}::{s[1]}"\n        return {\n            "promote_slots":             {_ser_slot(k): v for k, v in self.promote_slots.items()},\n            "retrograde_slots":          {_ser_slot(k): v for k, v in self.retrograde_slots.items()},\n            "prune_slots":               sorted(_ser_slot(s) for s in self.prune_slots),\n            "persistent_conflict_slots": sorted(_ser_slot(s) for s in self.persistent_conflict_slots),\n            "reinforcement_slots":       {\n                f"{e}::{f}::{v}": n for (e, f, v), n in self.reinforcement_slots.items()\n            },\n            "challenger_strength":       {_ser_slot(k): v for k, v in self.challenger_strength.items()},\n            "confidence":                self.confidence,\n            "raw_v15_7a_signals_ref":    dict(self.raw_v15_7a_signals_ref),\n        }\n\n\nclass LatentRationalMemoryReceptor:\n    """Translates LatentSignals (v15.7a adapter output) into LatentDecisionPressure.\n\n    Stateless across update calls (each call recomputes from scratch).\n    The Organism owns one instance; it calls update_from_signals at\n    end_episode and the resulting pressure is read on the next episode\'s\n    perceive().\n    """\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self.last_pressure: LatentDecisionPressure = LatentDecisionPressure.empty()\n        self.update_count: int = 0\n        self.history: list = []   # optional: list of (episode_id, pressure_snapshot)\n\n    def update_from_signals(\n        self,\n        signals: Any,                # LatentSignals (avoid hard import)\n        value_resolver: Callable[[str, int], Optional[str]],\n        episode_id: Optional[int] = None,\n    ) -> LatentDecisionPressure:\n        """Compute LatentDecisionPressure from a LatentSignals snapshot.\n\n        value_resolver(attr_family, value_idx) -> Optional[str]\n            The adapter\'s resolve_value_idx callable. Used to translate\n            v15.7a integer indices back to organism vocabulary so arbiters\n            can match against incoming text values.\n        """\n        self.update_count += 1\n        if signals is None or signals.is_empty():\n            self.last_pressure = LatentDecisionPressure.empty()\n            self.history.append((episode_id, self.last_pressure))\n            return self.last_pressure\n\n        promote_slots: Dict[Tuple[str, str], str] = {}\n        for slot, v_idx in signals.promote_candidate.items():\n            v_str = value_resolver(slot[1], v_idx)\n            if v_str is not None:\n                promote_slots[slot] = v_str\n\n        retrograde_slots: Dict[Tuple[str, str], str] = {}\n        for slot, v_idx in signals.retrograde_candidate.items():\n            v_str = value_resolver(slot[1], v_idx)\n            if v_str is not None:\n                retrograde_slots[slot] = v_str\n\n        prune_slots = set(signals.prune_candidate.keys())\n        persistent = set(signals.conflict_persistence)\n\n        reinforcement_slots: Dict[Tuple[str, str, str], float] = {}\n        for slot, val_to_count in signals.confirmation_count.items():\n            for v_idx, n in val_to_count.items():\n                if n >= 2:\n                    v_str = value_resolver(slot[1], v_idx)\n                    if v_str is not None:\n                        reinforcement_slots[(slot[0], slot[1], v_str)] = float(n)\n\n        challenger_strength = dict(signals.challenger_strength)\n\n        diag = signals.raw_v15_7a_signals or {}\n        n_audit = int(diag.get("audit_log_size", 0))\n        n_provisional = int(diag.get("n_provisional_entries", 0))\n        confidence = min(1.0, (n_audit + n_provisional * 0.5) / 30.0)\n\n        pressure = LatentDecisionPressure(\n            promote_slots=promote_slots,\n            retrograde_slots=retrograde_slots,\n            prune_slots=prune_slots,\n            persistent_conflict_slots=persistent,\n            reinforcement_slots=reinforcement_slots,\n            challenger_strength=challenger_strength,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            raw_v15_7a_signals_ref=dict(diag),\n        )\n        self.last_pressure = pressure\n        self.history.append((episode_id, pressure))\n        return pressure\n\n    def reset(self) -> None:\n        self.last_pressure = LatentDecisionPressure.empty()\n        self.update_count = 0\n        self.history = []\n\n\n__all__ = [\n    "LatentDecisionPressure",\n    "LatentRationalMemoryReceptor",\n]\n',
}

def write_fcem_v15_7a_engine() -> str:
    pkg = FCEM_ENGINE_DIR / "d_cortex"
    pkg.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    for _fname, _content in FCEM_V15_7A_FILES.items():
        (pkg / _fname).write_text(_content, encoding="utf-8")
    print(f"[FCEM] wrote real v15.7a d_cortex consolidator -> {pkg} ({len(FCEM_V15_7A_FILES)} files)", flush=True)
    return str(FCEM_ENGINE_DIR)


def ts() -> str:
    return time.strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", time.gmtime())


def ensure_dir(p: Path) -> Path:
    p.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return p


def run(cmd, cwd: Optional[Path] = None, env: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None, check: bool = True, timeout: Optional[int] = None) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess:
    print(f"[RUN] {' '.join(map(str, cmd))}", flush=True)
    cp = subprocess.run(
        list(map(str, cmd)),
        cwd=str(cwd) if cwd else None,
        env=env,
        text=True,
        stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
        stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
        timeout=timeout,
    )
    if cp.stdout.strip():
        print(cp.stdout[-5000:], flush=True)
    if cp.stderr.strip():
        print(cp.stderr[-5000:], file=sys.stderr, flush=True)
    if check and cp.returncode != 0:
        raise RuntimeError(f"Command failed rc={cp.returncode}: {cmd}\nSTDOUT:\n{cp.stdout}\nSTDERR:\n{cp.stderr}")
    return cp


def sha256_text(s: str) -> str:
    return hashlib.sha256(s.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()


def load_secret_key() -> str:
    key = os.environ.get("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", "").strip()
    if not key and IN_COLAB and userdata is not None:
        try:
            k = userdata.get("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY")
            if k:
                key = str(k).strip()
        except Exception as exc:
            print(f"[SECRET] Colab userdata unavailable: {exc}", flush=True)
    if not key:
        key = getpass.getpass("Paste ANTHROPIC_API_KEY, input is hidden: ").strip()
    if not key.startswith("sk-ant-"):
        raise RuntimeError("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY missing or not Anthropic-shaped. Use Colab Secret ANTHROPIC_API_KEY.")
    os.environ["ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"] = key
    return key


def safe_env() -> Dict[str, str]:
    env = os.environ.copy()
    env.update({
        "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY": os.environ["ANTHROPIC_API_KEY"],
        "LLM_PROVIDER": "anthropic",
        "LLM_MODEL": LLM_MODEL,
        "LLM_MAX_TOKENS": LLM_MAX_TOKENS,
        "LLM_TEMPERATURE": LLM_TEMPERATURE,
        "MEMORY_SERVICE_URL": MEMORY_SERVICE_URL,
        "MEMORY_STORAGE_PATH": str(MEMORY_STORAGE),
        "MEMORY_BACKEND": "hybrid",
        "FCEM_ENABLED": "true",
        "FCEM_CONSOLIDATE_EVERY_N": "3",
        "BYON_LEVEL3_FULL_ORGANISM_EXPERIMENT": "true",
        "D_CORTEX_V99_INTEGRATED": "true",
        "DCORTEX_V99_OUTPUT_DIR": str(RESULTS_DIR / "dcortex_v99_audit"),
        "D_CORTEX_V99_OUTPUT_DIR": str(RESULTS_DIR / "dcortex_v99_audit"),
        "FCEM_MEMORY_ENGINE_ROOT": str(FCEM_ENGINE_DIR),
        "FSOAT_REQUIRE_EXTERNAL_FCEM_RUNTIME": "true",
        "PYTHONUNBUFFERED": "1",
    })
    return env


def mount_drive_if_needed() -> None:
    if IN_COLAB and drive is not None:
        drive.mount("/content/drive", force_remount=False)
    ensure_dir(WORK_ROOT)
    ensure_dir(RESULTS_DIR)
    ensure_dir(MEMORY_STORAGE)
    ensure_dir(LOCAL_ROOT / "npm-cache")


def install_system_deps() -> None:
    print("[SETUP] installing Python dependencies", flush=True)
    run([PYTHON, "-m", "pip", "install", "-q", "--upgrade", "pip"], check=False, timeout=240)
    run([PYTHON, "-m", "pip", "install", "-q",
         "fastapi", "uvicorn[standard]", "pydantic", "numpy", "faiss-cpu", "sentence-transformers",
         "prometheus-client", "datasets", "tokenizers", "psutil"], check=True, timeout=900)


def clone_or_refresh_repo() -> None:
    if REPO_DIR.exists():
        git_dir = REPO_DIR / ".git"
        if not git_dir.exists():
            print(f"[REPO] removing non-git dir {REPO_DIR}", flush=True)
            shutil.rmtree(REPO_DIR)
        else:
            cp = run(["git", "status", "--porcelain"], cwd=REPO_DIR, check=False)
            if cp.returncode != 0:
                shutil.rmtree(REPO_DIR)
            else:
                run(["git", "fetch", "origin", REPO_BRANCH, "--depth", "1"], cwd=REPO_DIR, check=False)
                run(["git", "checkout", REPO_BRANCH], cwd=REPO_DIR, check=True)
                run(["git", "reset", "--hard", f"origin/{REPO_BRANCH}"], cwd=REPO_DIR, check=True)
    if not REPO_DIR.exists():
        ensure_dir(REPO_DIR.parent)
        run(["git", "clone", "--depth", "1", "--branch", REPO_BRANCH, REPO_URL, str(REPO_DIR)], check=True, timeout=900)
    commit = run(["git", "rev-parse", "HEAD"], cwd=REPO_DIR).stdout.strip()
    print(f"[REPO] official byon_optimus main commit={commit}", flush=True)


def repair_node_exec_permissions(orch: Path) -> None:
    """Repair executable bits for native npm binaries, and fail early if still not executable."""
    esbuild_bin = orch / "node_modules" / "@esbuild" / "linux-x64" / "bin" / "esbuild"
    run(["chmod", "-R", "u+rwX", str(orch / "node_modules")], cwd=orch, check=False, timeout=240)
    if esbuild_bin.exists():
        run(["chmod", "+x", str(esbuild_bin)], cwd=orch, check=False, timeout=60)
        probe = run([str(esbuild_bin), "--version"], cwd=orch, check=False, timeout=60)
        if probe.returncode != 0:
            raise RuntimeError(
                "esbuild is not executable. This usually means node_modules is on a noexec/FUSE mount. "
                f"Current repo path={REPO_DIR}. v9.9 expects it under /content, not Google Drive."
            )


def npm_install() -> None:
    orch = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator"
    env = os.environ.copy()
    env.update({
        "npm_config_cache": str(LOCAL_ROOT / "npm-cache"),
        "PLAYWRIGHT_SKIP_BROWSER_DOWNLOAD": "1",
    })
    run(["npm", "install", "--ignore-scripts"], cwd=orch, env=env, check=True, timeout=1200)
    repair_node_exec_permissions(orch)


def write_v99_source() -> Path:
    ms = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator" / "memory-service"
    dst = ms / "dcortex_v99_source.py"
    source = V99_SOURCE_RAW
    dst.write_text(source, encoding="utf-8")
    source_copy = RESULTS_DIR / "dcortex_v99_source.injected.py"
    source_copy.write_text(source, encoding="utf-8")
    print(f"[D_CORTEX] wrote full v9.9 source -> {dst} lines={source.count(chr(10))+1} sha256={sha256_text(source)}", flush=True)
    print(f"[D_CORTEX] persisted injected source copy -> {source_copy}", flush=True)
    # Fail before server startup if the injected raw source is syntactically invalid.
    run([PYTHON, "-m", "py_compile", str(dst)], check=True, timeout=120)
    return dst


def write_dcortex_adapter() -> Path:
    ms = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator" / "memory-service"
    adapter = ms / "dcortex_v99_adapter.py"
    adapter.write_text(ADAPTER_CODE, encoding="utf-8")
    print(f"[D_CORTEX] wrote adapter -> {adapter}", flush=True)
    return adapter


def patch_server_py() -> None:
    server = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator" / "memory-service" / "server.py"
    text = server.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    if "DCortexV99Adapter" not in text:
        text = text.replace("from fcem_backend import FcemBackend\n", "from fcem_backend import FcemBackend\nfrom dcortex_v99_adapter import DCortexV99Adapter\n")
        text = text.replace("fcem: Optional[FcemBackend] = None\n", "fcem: Optional[FcemBackend] = None\ndcortex_v99: Optional[DCortexV99Adapter] = None\n")
        text = text.replace("    global handlers, fcem, start_time\n", "    global handlers, fcem, dcortex_v99, start_time\n")
        marker = "    logger.info(\n        \"Memory backend mode: %s (FCE-M enabled=%s).\", backend_mode, fcem.enabled\n    )\n"
        inject = marker + "\n    # D_Cortex v9.9 additive memory organ, enabled by Colab integration patch.\n    # server.py is <repo>/byon-orchestrator/memory-service/server.py.\n    # parents[2] is the official byon_optimus repo root.\n    dcortex_v99 = DCortexV99Adapter(storage_path, str(Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]))\n    logger.info(\"D_Cortex v9.9 memory organ initialized: %s\", dcortex_v99.status())\n"
        if marker not in text:
            raise RuntimeError("server.py patch marker not found near FCE-M backend init")
        text = text.replace(marker, inject)
        action_marker = "    elif action == \"embed_batch\":\n        return await embed_texts(request)\n\n    else:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f\"Unknown action: {action}\")\n"
        action_inject = """    elif action == \"embed_batch\":
        return await embed_texts(request)

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    # D_Cortex v9.9 additive semantic grounded QA memory organ
    # ------------------------------------------------------------------
    elif action == \"dcortex_v99_status\":
        if dcortex_v99 is None:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=\"D_Cortex v9.9 adapter not initialized\")
        return {\"success\": True, \"dcortex_v99\": dcortex_v99.status()}

    elif action == \"dcortex_v99_run_audit\":
        if dcortex_v99 is None:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=\"D_Cortex v9.9 adapter not initialized\")
        return dcortex_v99.run_audit(
            fast_run=bool(request.get(\"fast_run\", False)),
            timeout_sec=int(request.get(\"timeout_sec\", 14400)),
        )

    elif action == \"dcortex_v99_grounding_packet\":
        if dcortex_v99 is None:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=\"D_Cortex v9.9 adapter not initialized\")
        return {\"success\": True, \"packet\": dcortex_v99.grounding_packet(request.get(\"query\"))}

    elif action == \"dcortex_v99_semantic_probe\":
        if dcortex_v99 is None:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=\"D_Cortex v9.9 adapter not initialized\")
        return dcortex_v99.semantic_probe(request.get(\"query\", \"\"))

    else:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f\"Unknown action: {action}\")
"""
        if action_marker not in text:
            raise RuntimeError("server.py action marker not found near embed_batch")
        text = text.replace(action_marker, action_inject)
    server.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")
    print(f"[PATCH] server.py patched for D_Cortex v9.9 actions: {', '.join(DCORTEX_SERVICE_ACTIONS)}", flush=True)


def write_live_e2e_script() -> Path:
    orch = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator"
    script = orch / "scripts" / "byon-dcortex-v99-live-e2e.mjs"
    script.write_text(E2E_CODE, encoding="utf-8")
    script.chmod(0o755)
    print(f"[D_CORTEX] wrote live E2E harness -> {script}", flush=True)
    return script


def start_memory_service(env: Dict[str, str]) -> subprocess.Popen:
    ms = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator" / "memory-service"
    log_path = RESULTS_DIR / "memory_service.log"
    print(f"[MEMORY] starting service at {MEMORY_SERVICE_URL} log={log_path}", flush=True)
    log_f = log_path.open("w", encoding="utf-8")
    p = subprocess.Popen(
        [PYTHON, "-u", "server.py"],
        cwd=str(ms),
        env=env,
        stdout=log_f,
        stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
        text=True,
    )
    import urllib.request
    deadline = time.time() + 180
    last_err = None
    while time.time() < deadline:
        if p.poll() is not None:
            raise RuntimeError(f"memory-service exited early rc={p.returncode}. Tail:\n{log_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')[-5000:]}")
        try:
            with urllib.request.urlopen(MEMORY_SERVICE_URL + "/health", timeout=3) as r:
                if r.status == 200:
                    print("[MEMORY] service healthy", flush=True)
                    return p
        except Exception as exc:
            last_err = exc
            time.sleep(3)
    raise RuntimeError(f"memory-service did not become healthy: {last_err}. Tail:\n{log_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')[-5000:]}")


def memory_post(payload: Dict[str, Any], timeout: int = 600) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    import urllib.request
    import urllib.error
    data = json.dumps(payload).encode("utf-8")
    req = urllib.request.Request(
        MEMORY_SERVICE_URL + "/",
        data=data,
        headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
        method="POST",
    )
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as resp:
            return json.loads(resp.read().decode("utf-8"))
    except urllib.error.HTTPError as exc:
        body = exc.read().decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
        log_tail = ""
        try:
            log_path = RESULTS_DIR / "memory_service.log"
            if log_path.exists():
                log_tail = log_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")[-12000:]
        except Exception as log_exc:
            log_tail = f"<could not read memory_service.log: {log_exc!r}>"
        raise RuntimeError(
            f"memory-service HTTP {exc.code} for action={payload.get('action')}\n"
            f"BODY:\n{body[-8000:]}\n\nMEMORY_SERVICE_LOG_TAIL:\n{log_tail}"
        ) from exc


def main() -> None:
    mount_drive_if_needed()
    write_fcem_v15_7a_engine()  # stage the REAL v15.7a FCE-M runtime before the service starts
    api_key = load_secret_key()
    print(f"[SECRET] Anthropic key loaded, prefix={api_key[:10]}..., length={len(api_key)}. It will not be written to disk.", flush=True)

    install_system_deps()
    clone_or_refresh_repo()
    npm_install()
    write_v99_source()
    write_dcortex_adapter()
    patch_server_py()
    write_live_e2e_script()

    orch = REPO_DIR / "byon-orchestrator"
    env = safe_env()
    run(["npm", "run", "build"], cwd=orch, env=env, check=False, timeout=900)
    if RUN_NPM_TEST:
        run(["npm", "test"], cwd=orch, env=env, check=False, timeout=1200)

    proc = None
    run_report: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "timestamp": ts(),
        "runner_version": "v9.9-repo-root-path-repair-full-raw",
        "repo_url": REPO_URL,
        "repo_branch": REPO_BRANCH,
        "repo_commit": run(["git", "rev-parse", "HEAD"], cwd=REPO_DIR).stdout.strip(),
        "runtime_repo_dir": str(REPO_DIR),
        "results_dir": str(RESULTS_DIR),
        "llm_model": LLM_MODEL,
        "api_key_written_to_disk": False,
        "dcortex_actions": DCORTEX_SERVICE_ACTIONS,
    }
    try:
        proc = start_memory_service(env)
        import urllib.request
        run_report["memory_health"] = json.loads(urllib.request.urlopen(MEMORY_SERVICE_URL + "/health", timeout=5).read().decode("utf-8"))
        run_report["dcortex_status_start"] = memory_post({"action": "dcortex_v99_status"}, timeout=30)

        if RUN_DCORTEX_V99:
            print("[D_CORTEX] running full v9.9 audit through BYON memory-service action", flush=True)
            run_report["dcortex_v99_run"] = memory_post({"action": "dcortex_v99_run_audit", "fast_run": False, "timeout_sec": 14400}, timeout=15000)
            if not run_report["dcortex_v99_run"].get("success", False):
                run_report["dcortex_v99_run_failed_but_captured"] = True
                dcr = run_report["dcortex_v99_run"]
                print("=" * 94, flush=True)
                print("[D_CORTEX] audit returned success=false", flush=True)
                print(f"[D_CORTEX] returncode={dcr.get('returncode')} duration={dcr.get('duration_sec')} log_path={dcr.get('log_path')}", flush=True)
                if dcr.get("error"):
                    print("[D_CORTEX] error:", str(dcr.get("error"))[-4000:], flush=True)
                if dcr.get("traceback"):
                    print("[D_CORTEX] traceback_tail:", str(dcr.get("traceback"))[-8000:], flush=True)
                if dcr.get("status"):
                    print("[D_CORTEX] adapter_status:", json.dumps(dcr.get("status"), indent=2)[-8000:], flush=True)
                print("[D_CORTEX] stdout_tail:", flush=True)
                print(str(dcr.get("stdout_tail", ""))[-12000:], flush=True)
                print("[D_CORTEX] stderr_tail:", flush=True)
                print(str(dcr.get("stderr_tail", ""))[-12000:], flush=True)
                raise RuntimeError("D_Cortex v9.9 audit returned success=false; diagnostic payload printed above and saved in report")
            run_report["dcortex_grounding_packet"] = memory_post({"action": "dcortex_v99_grounding_packet", "query": "BYON level and source grounding"}, timeout=60)

        if RUN_FSOAT:
            print("[FSOAT] running full-source organism activation, full mode, live Anthropic", flush=True)
            fsoat_env = env.copy()
            fsoat_env.update({
                "FSOAT_MODE": "full",
                "FSOAT_MEMORY_SERVICE_URL": MEMORY_SERVICE_URL,
                "FSOAT_DRY_RUN_EXECUTOR": os.environ.get("FSOAT_DRY_RUN_EXECUTOR", "true"),
                "FSOAT_RUN_ID": "colab-dcortex-v99-" + str(int(time.time())),
            })
            cp = run(["node", "scripts/byon-full-source-organism-activation-test.mjs"], cwd=orch, env=fsoat_env, check=False, timeout=1800)
            run_report["fsoat"] = {"returncode": cp.returncode, "stdout_tail": cp.stdout[-8000:], "stderr_tail": cp.stderr[-8000:]}
            if cp.returncode != 0:
                print("[FSOAT] failed; keeping report but continuing to D_Cortex live E2E if enabled", flush=True)

        if RUN_LIVE_BYON_DCORTEX_QA:
            print("[E2E] running BYON + D_Cortex live QA gating harness", flush=True)
            e2e_env = env.copy()
            e2e_out = RESULTS_DIR / "byon-dcortex-v99-live-e2e"
            e2e_env["BYON_DCORTEX_E2E_OUT"] = str(e2e_out)
            cp = run(["node", "scripts/byon-dcortex-v99-live-e2e.mjs"], cwd=orch, env=e2e_env, check=False, timeout=900)
            run_report["byon_dcortex_live_e2e"] = {"returncode": cp.returncode, "stdout_tail": cp.stdout[-8000:], "stderr_tail": cp.stderr[-8000:], "out_dir": str(e2e_out)}

        run_report["dcortex_status_final"] = memory_post({"action": "dcortex_v99_status"}, timeout=30)
        run_report["success"] = True
    except Exception as exc:
        run_report["success"] = False
        run_report["error"] = repr(exc)
        print(f"[FATAL] {exc}", flush=True)
    finally:
        if proc is not None and proc.poll() is None:
            print("[MEMORY] stopping service", flush=True)
            proc.terminate()
            try:
                proc.wait(timeout=20)
            except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
                proc.kill()
        report_path = RESULTS_DIR / "byon_dcortex_v99_full_selfcontained_colab_report.json"
        report_path.write_text(json.dumps(run_report, indent=2, default=str), encoding="utf-8")
        md_path = RESULTS_DIR / "byon_dcortex_v99_full_selfcontained_colab_summary.md"
        md_path.write_text(
            "# BYON + D_Cortex v9.9 full organism Colab run\n\n" +
            f"- timestamp: {run_report.get('timestamp')}\n" +
            f"- runner_version: {run_report.get('runner_version')}\n" +
            f"- runtime_repo_dir: {run_report.get('runtime_repo_dir')}\n" +
            f"- repo_commit: {run_report.get('repo_commit')}\n" +
            f"- model: {run_report.get('llm_model')}\n" +
            f"- success: {run_report.get('success')}\n" +
            f"- api_key_written_to_disk: {run_report.get('api_key_written_to_disk')}\n" +
            f"- report_json: {report_path}\n" +
            f"- results_dir: {RESULTS_DIR}\n",
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        print("=" * 94)
        print(f"[DONE] report -> {report_path}")
        print(f"[DONE] summary -> {md_path}")
        print("=" * 94)
        if not run_report.get("success"):
            raise SystemExit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
